Request Description
This endpoint is used to authenticate a user via HTTP POST request to https://restful-booker.herokuapp.com/auth. The request should include a payload with the raw request body type, containing the user's password. ### Request Body - `password`: (string) The user's password. ### Response Upon successful execution, the endpoint returns a status code of 200 and a response in JSON format with the following key: - `reason`: (string) An empty string indicating successful authentication.
